<date>1615709854955<//date>< Pictures>
[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOog69yZIcfw5Frmp03vTktruS_bnzmLGnEqc_U=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNr0vVQDe6PxXaIrJXINJvt-5jXdvC0avvFmm5j=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMpj_LSBTs6aPF-Eexbc9wTTY72qfFSG7Q-oXHr=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /Pictures>
<response>None<//response><text>Little disclaimer before we start: I'm Indonesian, came in a group of 5 (all Indos), 2 have roots from Kalimantan/Borneo, one of which is from Singkawang and the other from Pontianak (not far from Singkawang). I must emphasize, This Is The Bomb.

Main dishes we got:
- Bakmi Singkawang: literally my favorite bowl of noodles in the entire LA county, like seriously. The texture and the flavor is just so on point, it puts other Indonesian noodle shops to shame (*cough* West Covina). To be fair, it doesn't have the same taste as your average noodles because it does have a slight vinegar taste, but that complements the flavors this dish has to offer. Like usually I'm the type of person to drown my noods in soup (don't @ me) but this? Heck no, the flavors are just too perfect that it shines, even without the soup 10/10
- Kwetiau Goreng Singkawang: solid dish, the kwetiau has a mild wok flavor, and the toppings are just seasoned perfectly to complement those noodles. I'm personally not a kwetiau girl, would probably have chosen the mie goreng instead but it's okay because this is still fire.
- Sup Sayur Asin: we didn't order this soup but it came with two of our dishes mentioned above (I think). But, I kid you not, this is the best sayur asin I've had in a long long time, probably better than most I've had in Indo. It has a bit of pork pieces in the bottom and the veggies in it aren't smelly at all (it's common for the veggie to be smelly). Honestly I would come back just for this soup ngl
- Nasi Campur: it came with the thick clear gravy sauce (not sure what it's called) but if it doesn't, just ask for it. I loved this one but I think it's missing something, maybe the broth isn't salty enough? Maybe the rice wasn't soft enough? I'm not even sure. For those wondering: the pork belly was super fat (which I love) but I know not everyone is super into that.
- Nasi Capcai: super nostalgic because it tastes exactly like what I used to eat; the veggies are still a bit crunchy which I know some people prefer. Definitely one of the healthier options or if you want to eat more veggies.

Appetizers & Others:
- Hakong: 8/10 without the sauce, 10/10 with the sauce. Bruh. That sauce is magic I swear. It complements the hakong so well with some balanced sweetness, sourness, and savoriness. Without it, it needs just a touch more salt but I think it's meant to be eaten with the sauce, so I'm not complaining haha.
- Choi pan: according to my friends, these are not singkawang style, but it's super delicious nonetheless. The sauce is the one that came with our kwetiau but it's delicious and spicy, but not as watery as the one I'm used too. The filling itself is super flavorful (with quite a good amount of white pepper), the wrapper is kinda chewy/bouncy in a good way--and is not too thick.
- Es doger: omfg they have ketan singkong and kolang kaling in it!! They had some interesting stuffs in it like popping boba and lychee jelly I think but I don't really mind it lol. The drink part is not overwhelmingly sweet, just the right amount for this dessert (I'm sure they use Marjan syrup)
- Sambal terasi: if yall need more spicy, do ask for this. You're welcome.

General situation:
Came when LA had outdoor dining open, but not indoor (3/13). I heard they're going to have both indoor and outdoor next week. Their outdoor seating is a spacious patio with some heater to keep you warm. The owners and workers are all Indonesian, with the owners originally from Singkawang. I know they serve Thai food but we didn't really ask why nor try it. All of the utensils and plates were single use (paper plates to serve the food, styrofoam plates for us to share), except for the bowls used for the noodles and soups where they used legit noodle bowls.

TL;DR: they have awesome Indonesian food that everyone must try. If you think Borneo Kalimantan Cuisine is good, try this one and you'll be blown away. 10/10 would come back and bring my Indo and non-Indo friends and families here!!<//text></record>

Ambiance is good, food is good, price is good for the Indonesian food size (note: Indonesian food size is smaller than average American food size), parking was not an issue during dinner time, restaurant name was clearly visible from the street when I came after dark for dinner, customer service is great. I ordered Soto Betawi. It had a lot of meat--very fulfilling and tasty, almost like the one I tasted in Indonesia. They gave red bean dessert, which is a plus for Asian restaurant. I had a great experience.</Review>

< text>
If you are thinking about ordering takeout from Singkawang Cafe (they offer delivery via Uber Eats), my suggestion is to avoid this option. Actually, considering their rudeness and disregard for customer service, my suggestion would be to find an alternative location. Singkawang Cafe messed up an order of 6 items from Uber Eats, preparing only half the items ordered (total of 3/6 prepared). That's okay, people make mistakes. When I called, they said that they messed up the order, and apologized, they could clearly see the order chit which had six items on it. I was upset at this point because my wife and children were hungry and we had half of our order ready. But the icing on the cake was when we spoke to the restaurant management in person, they changed their story saying that it was Uber Eats that made the mistake, only sending half the order to them. It is this dishonesty that made me write this review. Mistakes made, yes, it happens. Lying about it to the customer to cover your mistakes, that's another story. All we asked for was for the restaurant to cover the delivery charge since we had to go pick up the order ourselves (we even told them restaurant credit would be fine), and we were refused. I've ordered from this restaurant several times previously, but this time would be our last. Very disappointing.</text>

<time>1564750922502< /time><rate>5<//rate>< Review>
I grew up going to Tijuana 3-4 times a month, spent weekends there as a teen on occasions. The food took me back to that era. From the smells to the flavors of the Al Pastor, th Carne Asada and the Fish tacos. Let's talk about that smoky, sweet heat of the roasted habanero sause. Then wash it down with some Delicious home made Horcharta (I'll be waiting for your recipe. Jk), the refreshing Jamaica, but the drink that took me by surprise was the kale/pineapple/ cucumber agua fresca (Tastes like Banana). Talk about thirst quenching and refreshing. When I'm in the area again, I'll be sure to stop bye, better yet. I'll be hoping they bring their food to theTemecula Valley area. BTW, the staff is friendly, and lively. Este Lugar esta al cien.<//Review>

<review>Warning: you may become addicted! If you appreciate a good authentic taco with fresh ingredients, this is your place. The tortillas are hand made and cooked to order, topped with clean meat and fresh condiments.

I ordered a shrimp taco and a barbacoa taco.  They were both different but equally tasty. This was probably some of the best barbacoa I have had. The shrimp taco was loaded with succulent shrimp, cabbage and a special sauce.

They also have vegetarian selections, and their kale water with chia seeds is very refreshing. If you like good food and great service, Street tacos and grill is the way to go!< /review></record>

< review>
Lets get this straight: I love NBC even though I dont care much for sweets/desserts.

This location is the closest to where I work and from time to time we get these at work for the whole team. They offer small, medium size cupcakes and even cakes that you can use for birthdays or occasions. Sure they are a bit on the pricier side but hey they are totally worth every penny. If you like cupcakes and havent tried this place yet, stop everything and just go there to try it out. Trust me, you wont regret it. My favorite at this location is the Red Velvet cupcake. I dont know if its their perfectly moist cupcake or their icing but it just melts in your mouth. I have tried a few of their other flavors and they also have different seasonal flavors and free samples at their store from time to time but for me, nothing beats red velvet, not even chocolate!

Parking in easy at this location and timings are also pretty decent for you to get a Bundtini any time of the day!< /review>

< Text>
In 2003, I bought my new Jeep Grand Cherokee from a different dealership on this lot.  I have only 56K miles on my Jeep to date.  I do a lot of my own service because of bad and poor experiences in the past.  The experience I have had at Lodi CDJR is one just as bad if not worse.  I originally took my Jeep in on 8/6/16 to have the air bag recall performed and to get an estimate for a check engine light.  (smog related).  For my jeep when it comes to smog issue, I want factory parts. Lodi CDJR furnishes a courtesy shuttle. (I need to rely on the courtesy vehicle because my Jeep is our only vehicle)  My Jeep was ready that day for pickup  (parts were ordered and I needed the vehicle ). I asked if the shuttle could pick me up. I was asked what time. I said 1 o'clock. They agreed.  I waited until 2:30 to call the dealer asking where my ride was. I was told they were just leaving.  I brought my Jeep in first thing Monday morning and got a ride home on the shuttle. At around 11:30 I was called saying my Jeep was ready.  I said I needed a ride. I was told they do not have anyone available at this time. They would call me when they did.  I waited until almost 3:30. I called the dealership back. I was told they just found someone that could get me. Then I waited another 45 minutes for the ride.  When I picked up my Jeep my front passenger door window was down about 4 inches and would not go up or down. Ended up being a repair I would have to do. They would not repair unless I paid to have it repaired.  All the windows were up when I left my vehicle that morning. My thought  is someone slammed the door that broke the cable on the regulator. The next day I tried no less than 6 times to call Robert, the service manager, who was always busy or not in. The operator told me I needed to leave  him a voice mail with my name and number and he would call me back. I left Robert  a voice mail with my name and number on 8/9/16 . I AM STILL WAITING AND IT IS MONDAY THE 15TH. Robert don't waste my time now with a phone call. My Jeep is a 2003 with low miles and very clean, at no time during any of the work being done was my seat covered with plastic to protect the vehicle seat from the dirty clothes of the mechanics.  My Jeep now gets 13.7 miles per gallon, it was getting 18.2 miles per gallon before they worked on it.  I will never buy, recommend or have any work done on any of my vehicles at Lodi CDJR.  I was thinking of buying a new Grand Cherokee Jeep and pass this one to one of my grand kids. If I do it will not be from this dealership.
For the mileage problem I found the cover from the air cleaner to the top of the fuel injection installed wrong. I reinstalled the cover and retrained the computer and now I have my good mileage back.  It is really to bad when the customer has to repair what the professionals work on. My personal recommendation use caution and think twice before dealing with Lodi CDJR.</Text>
